echo "QoS Policy Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    qos
        network-queue "nqNetwork" create
            description "Network Egress Queue"
            queue 1 create
                rate 100 cir 20
                mbs 100
                cbs 20
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            queue 2 best-effort create
                rate 100 cir 50
                cbs 50
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            queue 3 expedite create
                rate 100 cir 30
                cbs 30
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            queue 9 multipoint create
                mbs 50
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            queue 11 multipoint best-effort create
                cbs 20
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            queue 12 multipoint best-effort create
                rate 100 cir 50
                cbs 50
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            queue 13 multipoint expedite create
                rate 100 cir 30
                cbs 30
                high-prio-only 10
            exit
            fc be create
                multicast-queue 11
                queue 1
                egress-hsmda
                    queue 1
                exit
            exit
            fc ef create
                multicast-queue 12
                queue 2
                egress-hsmda
                    queue 6
                exit
            exit
            fc h2 create
                multicast-queue 13
                queue 3
                egress-hsmda
                    queue 5
                exit
            exit
        exit
        slope-policy "spDrop" create
            description "drop profile"
            high-slope
                start-avg 80
                max-avg 95
                max-prob 10
                no shutdown
            exit
            low-slope
                start-avg 30
                max-avg 95
                max-prob 20
                no shutdown
            exit
            time-average-factor 9
        exit
    exit

echo "CPM Filter Router and Svc-id Match Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    system
        security
            cpm-filter
                ip-filter
                    no shutdown
                    entry 600
                        match protocol tcp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 601
                        match protocol tcp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 608
                        match protocol tcp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 609
                        match protocol tcp
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 1000
                        match 
                            router Base
                        exit
                    exit
                exit
                mac-filter
                    no shutdown
                exit
            exit
        exit
    exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "Router (Service Side) Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    router Base
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "ISIS Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
        isis 0
            no shutdown
        exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "PIM Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
        pim
            no shutdown
        exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "Policy Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
        policy-options
            begin
            prefix-list "system1"
                prefix 125.123.0.0/24 prefix-length-range 32-32
            exit
            prefix-list "plHostRoute"
                prefix 0.0.0.0/0 prefix-length-range 32-32
            exit
            prefix-list "local-address"
                prefix 1.1.1.1/32 exact
                prefix 1.1.1.2/32 exact
                prefix 1.1.1.3/32 exact
                prefix 1.1.1.4/32 exact
                prefix 1.1.1.5/32 exact
            exit
            prefix-list "plDefaultRoute"
                prefix 0.0.0.0/0 exact
            exit
            prefix-list "plPrivateRoute"
                prefix 10.0.0.0/24 longer
                prefix 172.16.0.0/12 longer
                prefix 192.168.0.0/16 longer
            exit
            community "sifaju" members "target:64753:1015000"
            community "cmJXMAN" members "64753:1503" "64753:61023"
            community "sinopec" members "target:64753:1018000"
            community "xiaofang" members "target:64753:1014000"
            community "zjZhongChen" members "target:64753:1021000"
            community "ZhongXinYinHang" members "target:64753:1017000"
            community "jxRenMinYinHang" members "target:64753:1019000"
            policy-statement "direct2ospf"
                entry 10
                    from
                        protocol direct
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol ospf
                    exit
                    action accept
                        type 1
                    exit
                exit
                entry 20
                    from
                        protocol static
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol ospf
                    exit
                    action accept
                        type 1
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "label-filter"
                entry 10
                    from
                        prefix-list "system1"
                    exit
                    action accept
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "sifaju_export"
                entry 10
                    action accept
                        community add "sifaju"
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "sifaju_import"
                entry 10
                    from
                        protocol bgp-vpn
                        community "sifaju"
                    exit
                    action accept
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "rpSET_COMM_OUT"
                entry 10
                    from
                        prefix-list "plDefaultRoute"
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol bgp
                    exit
                    action reject
                exit
                entry 20
                    from
                        prefix-list "plPrivateRoute"
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol bgp
                    exit
                    action reject
                exit
                entry 30
                    from
                        protocol direct
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol bgp
                    exit
                    action accept
                        community replace "cmJXMAN"
                    exit
                exit
                entry 40
                    from
                        protocol static
                        tag 100
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol bgp
                    exit
                    action accept
                        community replace "cmJXMAN"
                        next-hop-self
                    exit
                exit
            exit
            policy-statement "rpStaticToISIS"
                entry 10
                    from
                        protocol static
                        tag 10
                    exit
                    to
                        protocol isis
                    exit
                    action accept
